\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
\begin{DoxyVerb}Represents something that may be installed later on, may have information
about where to fetch the relevant requirement and also contains logic for
installing the said requirement.
\end{DoxyVerb}
 

Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{req__install_8py_source_l00064}{64}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{req__install_8py_source}{req\+\_\+install.\+py}}.

\begin{DoxyVerb}Ensure that a source_dir is set.

This will create a temporary build dir if the name of the requirement
isn't known yet.

:param parent_dir: The ideal pip parent_dir for the source_dir.
    Generally src_dir for editables and build_dir for sdists.
:return: self.source_dir
\end{DoxyVerb}

\begin{DoxyVerb}Return whether any known-good hashes are specified as options.

References \mbox{\hyperlink{req__install_8py_source_l00149}{Install\+Requirement.\+hash\+\_\+options}}.

\Hypertarget{classpip_1_1__internal_1_1req_1_1req__install_1_1InstallRequirement_a6443a3bec25bb919f2624ae093fe645d}\label{classpip_1_1__internal_1_1req_1_1req__install_1_1InstallRequirement_a6443a3bec25bb919f2624ae093fe645d} 
\index{InstallRequirement@{InstallRequirement}!hashes@{hashes}}
\index{hashes@{hashes}!InstallRequirement@{InstallRequirement}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{hashes()}{hashes()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily  \mbox{\hyperlink{classpip_1_1__internal_1_1utils_1_1hashes_1_1Hashes}{Hashes}} hashes (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{self,  }\item[{bool }]{trust\+\_\+internet = {\ttfamily True} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyVerb}Return a hash-comparer that considers my option- and URL-based
hashes to be known-good.

Hashes in URLs--ones embedded in the requirements file, not ones
downloaded from an index server--are almost peers with ones from
flags. They satisfy --require-hashes (whether it was implicitly or
explicitly activated) but do not activate it. md5 and sha224 are not
allowed in flags, which should nudge people toward good algos. We
always OR all hashes together, even ones from URLs.

:param trust_internet: Whether to trust URL-based (#md5=...) hashes
    downloaded from the internet, as by populate_link()\end{DoxyVerb}
 

Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{req__install_8py_source_l00285}{285}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{req__install_8py_source}{req\+\_\+install.\+py}}.

or as a setup.py or a setup.cfg

{\footnotesize\ttfamily  \mbox{\hyperlink{prime__search_8m_a6f6ccfcf58b31cb6412107d9d5281426}{None}} load\+\_\+pyproject\+\_\+toml (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{self }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyVerb}Load the pyproject.toml file.

After calling this routine, all of the attributes related to PEP 517
processing for this requirement have been set. In particular, the
use_pep517 attribute can be used to determine whether we should
follow the PEP 517 or legacy (setup.py) code path.
\end{DoxyVerb}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily  \mbox{\hyperlink{prime__search_8m_a6f6ccfcf58b31cb6412107d9d5281426}{None}} prepare\+\_\+metadata (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{self }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyVerb}Ensure that project metadata is available.

Under PEP 517 and PEP 660, call the backend hook to prepare the metadata.
Under legacy processing, call setup.py egg-info.
\end{DoxyVerb}
 

Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{req__install_8py_source_l00540}{540}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{req__install_8py_source}{req\+\_\+install.\+py}}.

\index{InstallRequirement@{InstallRequirement}!uninstall@{uninstall}}
\index{uninstall@{uninstall}!InstallRequirement@{InstallRequirement}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{uninstall()}{uninstall()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily  Optional\mbox{[}\mbox{\hyperlink{classpip_1_1__internal_1_1req_1_1req__uninstall_1_1UninstallPathSet}{Uninstall\+Path\+Set}}\mbox{]} uninstall (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{self,  }\item[{bool }]{auto\+\_\+confirm = {\ttfamily False},  }\item[{bool }]{verbose = {\ttfamily False} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyVerb}Uninstall the distribution currently satisfying this requirement.

Prompts before removing or modifying files unless
``auto_confirm`` is True.

Refuses to delete or modify files outside of ``sys.prefix`` -
thus uninstallation within a virtual environment can only
modify that virtual environment, even if the virtualenv is
linked to global site-packages.\end{DoxyVerb}
